static font

Inria Serif Light Regular (InriaSerif-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSerif-Light', Everything looks good.

Pass

Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. Inria Serif Light Regular (InriaSerif-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Inria Serif' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Inria Serif Light'.

Pass

Inria Serif Light Italic (InriaSerif-LightItalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSerif-LightItalic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Inria Serif Light Italic (InriaSerif-LightItalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Inria Serif' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light Italic' = NID 1 'Inria Serif Light' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Pass

Inria Serif Regular (InriaSerif-Regular.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSerif-Regular', Everything looks good.

Pass

Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. Inria Serif Italic (InriaSerif-Italic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSerif-Italic', Everything looks good.

Inria Serif Bold (InriaSerif-Bold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSerif-Bold', Everything looks good.

Pass

Inria Serif Bold Italic (InriaSerif-BoldItalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'InriaSerif-BoldItalic', Everything looks good.

Pass

post

PostScript names

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Every PostScript name is fine.
